\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{server\+:}} Deprecated `require(\textquotesingle{}karma').server.\+start(){\ttfamily and}require(\textquotesingle{}karma\textquotesingle{}).Server.\+start()\`{} variants were removed from the public API. Instead use canonical form\+:
\end{DoxyItemize}


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ \{\ Server\ \}\ =\ require('karma');}
\DoxyCodeLine{const\ server\ =\ new\ Server();}
\DoxyCodeLine{server.start();}

\end{DoxyCode}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{cli\+:}} Karma is more strict and will error out if unknown option or argument is passed to CLI.
\item Using Karma to run Dart code in the browser is no longer supported. Use your favorite Dart-\/to-\/\+JS compiler instead.
\end{DoxyItemize}

{\ttfamily dart} file type has been removed without a replacement.

{\ttfamily custom\+File\+Handlers} DI token has been removed. Use \href{https://karma-runner.github.io/5.2/config/configuration-file.html\#middleware}{\texttt{ {\ttfamily middleware}}} to achieve similar functionality.

{\ttfamily custom\+Script\+Types} DI token has been removed. It had no effect, so no replacement is provided.
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\bfseries{deps\+:}} Some projects have socket.\+io tests that are version sensitive.
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11427}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/compare/v5.2.2...v5.2.3}{\texttt{ 5.\+2.\+3}} (2020-\/09-\/25)}{\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/compare/v5.2.2...v5.2.3}{\texttt{ 5.\+2.\+3}} (2020-\/09-\/25)}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11427}

As a result, all {\ttfamily custom\+Context\+File} and {\ttfamily custom\+Debug\+File} options much update their format to match this new format.

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The public api interface has changed to a constructor form. To upgrade change


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ server\ =\ require(karma).server}
\DoxyCodeLine{server.start(config,\ done)}

\end{DoxyCode}


to


\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ Server\ =\ require(karma).Server}
\DoxyCodeLine{var\ server\ =\ new\ Server(config,\ done)}
\DoxyCodeLine{server.start()}

\end{DoxyCode}


Closes \#1037, \#1482, \#1467 (\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/commit/82cbbadd}{\texttt{ 82cbbadd}})
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item Karma does not ship with any plugin. You need to explicitly install all the plugins you need. {\ttfamily karma init} can help with this.
\end{DoxyItemize}

Removed plugins that need to be installed explicitly are\+:


\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item karma-\/jasmine
\item karma-\/requirejs
\item karma-\/coffee-\/preprocessor
\item karma-\/html2js-\/preprocessor
\item karma-\/chrome-\/launcher
\item karma-\/firefox-\/launcher
\item karma-\/phantomjs-\/launcher
\item karma-\/script-\/launcher (\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/commit/e033d5618a98e1f83323bb650e0eaf89c339e5b5}{\texttt{ e033d561}})
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item remove {\ttfamily karma} binary in favor of karma-\/cli (\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/commit/c7d46270aca83ecfe78f69fa923bc574c0b5bfdc}{\texttt{ c7d46270}})
\item {\bfseries{config\+:}} log if no config file is specified (\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/commit/ce4c5646dfff7bd40abfd1f9e51dc4f5b779bf4a}{\texttt{ ce4c5646}})
\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11716}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11716}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item The {\ttfamily karma} module does not export {\ttfamily karma} binary anymore. The recommended way is to have local modules (karma and all the plugins that your project needs) stored in your {\ttfamily package.\+json}. You can run that particular Karma by {\ttfamily ./node\+\_\+modules/karma/bin/karma}. Or you can have {\ttfamily karma-\/cli} installed globally on your system, which enables you to use the {\ttfamily karma} command.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The global {\ttfamily karma} command (installed by {\ttfamily karma-\/cli}) does look for local version of Karma (including parent directories) first and fall backs to a global one.

The {\ttfamily bin/karma} binary does not look for any other instances of Karma and just runs the one that it belongs to.

(\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/commit/c7d46270aca83ecfe78f69fa923bc574c0b5bfdc}{\texttt{ c7d46270}})

\end{DoxyItemize}\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11760}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11760}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item reporters, launchers, preprocessors, adapters are separate plugins now, in order to use them, you need to install the npm package (probably add it as a {\ttfamily dev\+Dependency} into your {\ttfamily package.\+json}) and load in the {\ttfamily karma.\+conf.\+js} with `plugins = \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}karma-\/jasmine', ...\mbox{]}\`{}. Karma ships with couple of default plugins (karma-\/jasmine, karma-\/chrome-\/launcher, karma-\/phantomjs-\/launcher).
\item frameworks (such as jasmine, mocha, qunit) are configured using `frameworks = \mbox{[}\textquotesingle{}jasmine'\mbox{]};{\ttfamily instead of prepending}JASMINE\+\_\+\+ADAPTER\`{} into files.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\label{_v0.8.0}%
 \hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11761}{}\doxysubsection{\texorpdfstring{v0.\+8.\+0 (2013-\/03-\/18)}{v0.\+8.\+0 (2013-\/03-\/18)}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11761}
\hypertarget{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11762}{}\doxysubsubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Breaking Changes}{Breaking Changes}}\label{md__d_1_2_g_i_t_2_food_link_2foodlink_8client_2node__modules_2karma_2_c_h_a_n_g_e_l_o_g_autotoc_md11762}

\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item rename the project to "{}\+Karma"{}\+:
\item whenever you call the "{}testacular"{} binary, change it to "{}karma"{}, eg. {\ttfamily testacular start} becomes {\ttfamily karma start}.
\item if you rely on default name of the config file, change it to {\ttfamily karma.\+conf.\+js}.
\item if you access {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+testacular\+\_\+\+\_\+} object in the client code, change it to {\ttfamily \+\_\+\+\_\+karma\+\_\+\+\_\+}, eg. {\ttfamily window.\+\_\+\+\_\+testacular\+\_\+\+\_\+.\+files} becomes {\ttfamily window.\+\_\+\+\_\+karma\+\_\+\+\_\+.\+files}. (\href{https://github.com/karma-runner/karma/commit/026a20f7b467eb3b39c68ed509acc06e5dad58e6}{\texttt{ 026a20f7}})
\end{DoxyItemize}
